    SELECT p."ID_PRESUPUESTO", p."DESCUENTO", p."EXMIR_IVA", p."FECHA_PRESUPUESTO", p."FECHA_CREACION", p."ID_CLIENTE", p."ID_ESTADO", p."ID_FACTURA", p."TOTAL_PRESUPUESTO", c."ID_CLIENTE" AS "ID_CLIENTE0", c."CONTACTO", c."CUIT", c."DOMICILIO", c."ID_CONDICION_AFIP", c."LOCALIDAD", c."PROVINCIA", c."RAZON_SOCIAL", c."TELEFONO", c."TRANSPORTE", c."VALIDO", e."ID_ESTADO" AS "ID_ESTADO0", e."CODIGO", e."DESCRIPCION"
    FROM "PRESUPUESTO" AS p
    INNER JOIN "CLIENTE" AS c ON p."ID_CLIENTE" = c."ID_CLIENTE"
    INNER JOIN "ESTADO_PRESUPUESTO" AS e ON p."ID_ESTADO" = e."ID_ESTADO"
    WHERE p."ID_PRESUPUESTO" = @__id_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT a."ID_ARTICULO_PRESUPUESTO", a."CANTIDAD", a."PENDIENTE", a."CODIGO", a."DESCRIPCION", a."DESCUENTO", a."FECHA_CREACION", a."HAY_STOCK", a."ID_ARTICULO", a."ID_PRESUPUESTO", a."PRECIO_UNITARIO", a0."ID_ARTICULO" AS "ID_ARTICULO0", a0."CODIGO" AS "CODIGO0", a0."DESCRIPCION" AS "DESCRIPCION0", a0."HABILITADO", a0."ID_ARTICULO_PRECIO", a0."ID_ASOCIADO_RELLENO", a0."ID_COLOR", a0."ID_FABRICANTE", a0."ID_MEDIDA", a0."ID_SUBFAMILIA", a0."STOCK", c0."ID_COLOR" AS "ID_COLOR0", c0."CODIGO" AS "CODIGO1", c0."HEXA", c0."DESCRIPCION" AS "DESCRIPCION1", m."ID_MEDIDA" AS "ID_MEDIDA0", m."CODIGO" AS "CODIGO2", m."DESCRIPCION" AS "DESCRIPCION2", a1."ID_ARTICULO_PRECIO" AS "ID_ARTICULO_PRECIO0", a1."CODIGO" AS "CODIGO3", a1."DESCRIPCION" AS "DESCRIPCION3", a1."PRECIO1", a1."PRECIO2", a1."PRECIO3", a1."RELLENO", s."ID_SUBFAMILIA" AS "ID_SUBFAMILIA0", s."CODIGO" AS "CODIGO4", s."DESCRIPCION" AS "DESCRIPCION4"
    FROM "ARTICULO_PRESUPUESTO" AS a
    INNER JOIN "ARTICULO" AS a0 ON a."ID_ARTICULO" = a0."ID_ARTICULO"
    INNER JOIN "COLOR" AS c0 ON a0."ID_COLOR" = c0."ID_COLOR"
    INNER JOIN "MEDIDA" AS m ON a0."ID_MEDIDA" = m."ID_MEDIDA"
    LEFT JOIN "ARTICULO_PRECIO" AS a1 ON a0."ID_ARTICULO_PRECIO" = a1."ID_ARTICULO_PRECIO"
    LEFT JOIN "SUBFAMILIA" AS s ON a0."ID_SUBFAMILIA" = s."ID_SUBFAMILIA"
) AS t0 ON t."ID_PRESUPUESTO" = t0."ID_PRESUPUESTO"
ORDER BY t."ID_PRESUPUESTO", t."ID_CLIENTE0", t."ID_ESTADO0", t0."ID_ARTICULO_PRESUPUESTO", t0."ID_ARTICULO0", t0."ID_COLOR0", t0."ID_MEDIDA0", t0."ID_ARTICULO_PRECIO0"
